			}
			182 = {
				if = { 
					limit = {
						free_building_slots = {
							building = dockyard
							size > 1
							include_locked = yes
						}
					}
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 3
					add_building_construction = {
						type = dockyard
						level = 3
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
			}	
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					owns_state = 183 
				}		
				183 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							free_building_slots = {
								building = dockyard
								size > 1
								include_locked = yes
							}
						}
					}	
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 3
					add_building_construction = {
						type = dockyard
						level = 3
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					owns_state = 164 
				}
				164 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							free_building_slots = {
								building = dockyard
								size > 0
								include_locked = yes
							}
						}
					}	
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 3
					add_building_construction = {
						type = dockyard
						level = 3
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					NOT = { 
						owns_state = 183
						owns_state = 164
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_making_use_of_our_islands_tt
			}	
			else_if = { 
				limit = { 
					NOT = { 
						owns_state = 164
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_making_use_of_our_islands_dodecanese_tt
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { 
					NOT = { 
						owns_state = 183
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_making_use_of_our_islands_cyprus_tt
			}
			hidden_effect = { 
				if = { 
					limit = { 
						183 = { is_owned_by = GRE }
						NOT = { 183 = { is_core_of = GRE } }
					}
					add_state_core = 183
				}
			}
		}

				limit = {
					has_country_leader = {

					limit = {

		}
